But your body is your business and your body isn't a machine. Your business, it can't be a robot. You're a creator, you know, a human. And just like the natural world, you have rhythms, cycles, seasons, all of it. And ignoring those seasons doesn't make you stronger. just makes you burnt out. Some signs you might be kind of trapped in this hustle mode concept or this hustle mode period is when you feel guilt when you take time off. When you're filming and your content starts to feel forced, when you're constantly feeling behind just forever with no way out, and when you're growing resentment towards the business you're in. If any of that sounds familiar, you're not failing. You're just farming without the calendar. And here's what it means to work in seasons. Okay? There's number one, planting season, then two, growing season. Then three, harvest season. Then four, resting season. Now, let's break down exactly what these seasons look like. Planting season, the energy is quiet and strategic and low output and high focus. So the activities during planting season might be researching trends, doing market research, building systems or workflows for yourself, prepping a new series or themes or offers, and setting long-term goals for yourself. And the mindset during planting season is going to be not much revenue yet, but trust that growth is coming. And this is the season most people rush through, and it's a mistake. One tip that I would offer is to block off one full week each quarter to plan strategy batch film or rebuild content systems that you have established. Now, growing season, the energy in growing season is high creativity, consistent posting, momentum building. The activities are going to look like filming and posting and launching content, testing offers, bundles, promos, um showing up daily with intention. You're in the DMs. You're active. You're online and you're building visibility. You're going to be posting to social, trying to do high visibility things, Tik Toks, reals, things of that nature. And your mindset is that you are putting in effort before major returns. This is where you want to stay focused because this is where habits lock in. And a tip I'd offer in this period is to run a 30-day sprint here. Schedule content one week at a time to just maintain clarity and motivation, but the sprint is 30 days. And that brings you to harvest season. The energy in harvest season is going to be high reward, high conversion, less output, more return. The activities are going to look like launching the series or bundles that you've been promoting. It's going to look like promoting evergreen content. So, if there's a holiday or theme you're in the midst of, you can pull that evergreen content and reuse it. The activities are going to also look like banking on previous work. So recycling content that performs well. It's also going to look like raising prices and maximizing LTV, the lifetime value of your customers, your fans, your subscribers. And the mindset during harvest season is you're working smarter and not harder. And the systems you built prior are now paying off. The tip I'd give you during this season is to set monthly harvest weeks where you can resell and repackage or promote your bestsellers with minimal new filming. And then that brings us to resting season. So this is where your energy becomes kind of low visibility, deep restoration, mental reset, you know, batteries recharging. Your activities are going to be things like taking off time from social media or from filming, sitting back and reviewing your analytics, any personal care or mental wellness, maybe a vacation. You're going to recharge your creative energy in this period. In the mindset, it should feel like yeah, you are still being productive, just not externally. And growth comes from rest. We all know that. My tip for you during this restorative or rest season is to schedule rest seasons before you burn out. Choose two to four weeks per year where output is intentionally low. The key is to know your season before your season decides for you. Ask yourself, am I in idea mode or execution mode? Am I launching things or refining things? Am I exhausted or energized? Do I need structure or do I need space? And there's no bad season, but there is misalignment. Most creators, they try to launch during a rest season or scale during a planting season. And that friction or that dissonance, it can add to burnout.
